    async def test_token_refresh_issues_new_tokens_and_revokes_old(
        self, async_client: AsyncClient, db_session: AsyncSession
    ):
        """Refresh token rotation: old token is revoked, new tokens issued."""
        user, password = await create_user_in_db(db_session, email="refresh@example.com")
        await db_session.commit()
    
        login_resp = await async_client.post(
            "/api/v1/auth/login",
            json={"email": user.email, "password": password},
        )
        assert login_resp.status_code == 200
        original_refresh = login_resp.json()["refresh_token"]
    
        refresh_resp = await async_client.post(
            "/api/v1/auth/refresh",
            json={"refresh_token": original_refresh},
        )
        assert refresh_resp.status_code == 200
        new_data = refresh_resp.json()

self = <app.domains.products.service.ProductService object at 0x726b3ef48a70>
category_id = None, search = 'hiking', min_price = None, max_price = None
in_stock = None, sort_by = None, sort_order = 'desc', page = 1, page_size = 20

    async def list_products(
        self,
        *,
        category_id: Optional[UUID] = None,
        search: Optional[str] = None,
        min_price: Optional[float] = None,
        max_price: Optional[float] = None,
        in_stock: Optional[bool] = None,
        sort_by: str = "created_at",
        sort_order: str = "desc",
        page: int = 1,
        page_size: int = 20,
    ) -> ProductList:
        filters = []
    
        if category_id is not None:
            filters.append(Product.category_id == category_id)
    
        if search:
            term = f"%{search.lower()}%"
            filters.append(
                func.lower(Product.name).like(term)
                | func.lower(Product.description).like(term)
            )
    
        if min_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price >= min_price)
    
        if max_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price <= max_price)
    
        if in_stock is True:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity > 0)
        elif in_stock is False:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity == 0)
    
        count_stmt = select(func.count()).select_from(Product)
        if filters:
            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(and_(*filters))
    
        count_result = await self.db.execute(count_stmt)
        total = count_result.scalar_one()
    
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        if filters:
            stmt = stmt.where(and_(*filters))

    async def list_products(
        self,
        *,
        category_id: Optional[UUID] = None,
        search: Optional[str] = None,
        min_price: Optional[float] = None,
        max_price: Optional[float] = None,
        in_stock: Optional[bool] = None,
        sort_by: str = "created_at",
        sort_order: str = "desc",
        page: int = 1,
        page_size: int = 20,
    ) -> ProductList:
        filters = []
    
        if category_id is not None:
            filters.append(Product.category_id == category_id)
    
        if search:
            term = f"%{search.lower()}%"
            filters.append(
                func.lower(Product.name).like(term)
                | func.lower(Product.description).like(term)
            )
    
        if min_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price >= min_price)
    
        if max_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price <= max_price)
    
        if in_stock is True:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity > 0)
        elif in_stock is False:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity == 0)
    
        count_stmt = select(func.count()).select_from(Product)
        if filters:
            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(and_(*filters))
    
        count_result = await self.db.execute(count_stmt)
        total = count_result.scalar_one()
    
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        if filters:
            stmt = stmt.where(and_(*filters))

    async def list_products(
        self,
        *,
        category_id: Optional[UUID] = None,
        search: Optional[str] = None,
        min_price: Optional[float] = None,
        max_price: Optional[float] = None,
        in_stock: Optional[bool] = None,
        sort_by: str = "created_at",
        sort_order: str = "desc",
        page: int = 1,
        page_size: int = 20,
    ) -> ProductList:
        filters = []
    
        if category_id is not None:
            filters.append(Product.category_id == category_id)
    
        if search:
            term = f"%{search.lower()}%"
            filters.append(
                func.lower(Product.name).like(term)
                | func.lower(Product.description).like(term)
            )
    
        if min_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price >= min_price)
    
        if max_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price <= max_price)
    
        if in_stock is True:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity > 0)
        elif in_stock is False:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity == 0)
    
        count_stmt = select(func.count()).select_from(Product)
        if filters:
            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(and_(*filters))
    
        count_result = await self.db.execute(count_stmt)
        total = count_result.scalar_one()
    
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        if filters:
            stmt = stmt.where(and_(*filters))

_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

self = <app.domains.products.service.ProductService object at 0x726b3eb9a540>
category_id = None, search = None, min_price = None, max_price = None
in_stock = None, sort_by = None, sort_order = 'desc', page = 1, page_size = 20

    async def list_products(
        self,
        *,
        category_id: Optional[UUID] = None,
        search: Optional[str] = None,
        min_price: Optional[float] = None,
        max_price: Optional[float] = None,
        in_stock: Optional[bool] = None,
        sort_by: str = "created_at",
        sort_order: str = "desc",
        page: int = 1,
        page_size: int = 20,
    ) -> ProductList:
        filters = []
    
        if category_id is not None:
            filters.append(Product.category_id == category_id)
    
        if search:
            term = f"%{search.lower()}%"
            filters.append(
                func.lower(Product.name).like(term)
                | func.lower(Product.description).like(term)
            )
    
        if min_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price >= min_price)
    
        if max_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price <= max_price)
    
        if in_stock is True:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity > 0)
        elif in_stock is False:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity == 0)
    
        count_stmt = select(func.count()).select_from(Product)
        if filters:
            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(and_(*filters))
    
        count_result = await self.db.execute(count_stmt)
        total = count_result.scalar_one()
    
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        if filters:
            stmt = stmt.where(and_(*filters))

self = <app.domains.products.service.ProductService object at 0x726b3f415d00>
category_id = None, search = None, min_price = None, max_price = None
in_stock = None, sort_by = None, sort_order = 'desc', page = 1, page_size = 2

    async def list_products(
        self,
        *,
        category_id: Optional[UUID] = None,
        search: Optional[str] = None,
        min_price: Optional[float] = None,
        max_price: Optional[float] = None,
        in_stock: Optional[bool] = None,
        sort_by: str = "created_at",
        sort_order: str = "desc",
        page: int = 1,
        page_size: int = 20,
    ) -> ProductList:
        filters = []
    
        if category_id is not None:
            filters.append(Product.category_id == category_id)
    
        if search:
            term = f"%{search.lower()}%"
            filters.append(
                func.lower(Product.name).like(term)
                | func.lower(Product.description).like(term)
            )
    
        if min_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price >= min_price)
    
        if max_price is not None:
            filters.append(Product.price <= max_price)
    
        if in_stock is True:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity > 0)
        elif in_stock is False:
            filters.append(Product.stock_quantity == 0)
    
        count_stmt = select(func.count()).select_from(Product)
        if filters:
            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(and_(*filters))
    
        count_result = await self.db.execute(count_stmt)
        total = count_result.scalar_one()
    
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        if filters:
            stmt = stmt.where(and_(*filters))

product_id = UUID('cc5bbe9b-eef3-4b8b-ab3d-892d069d0479')

    async def get_product(self, product_id: UUID) -> ProductRead:
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .where(Product.id == product_id)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        result = await self.db.execute(stmt)
        product = result.scalar_one_or_none()
    
        if product is None:
            raise NotFoundError(f"Product with id '{product_id}' not found.")

product_id = UUID('86b9e70d-ae3d-4cf0-b082-6d4564b54ed2')

    async def get_product(self, product_id: UUID) -> ProductRead:
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .where(Product.id == product_id)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        result = await self.db.execute(stmt)
        product = result.scalar_one_or_none()
    
        if product is None:
            raise NotFoundError(f"Product with id '{product_id}' not found.")

product_id = UUID('0c2fbabb-8ad7-43d9-9465-359381340ed7')

    async def get_product(self, product_id: UUID) -> ProductRead:
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .where(Product.id == product_id)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        result = await self.db.execute(stmt)
        product = result.scalar_one_or_none()
    
        if product is None:
            raise NotFoundError(f"Product with id '{product_id}' not found.")

self = <app.domains.products.service.ProductService object at 0x726b3e93a510>
product_id = UUID('b0298810-e623-4dbc-9051-71f7d25d0388')

    async def get_product(self, product_id: UUID) -> ProductRead:
        stmt = (
            select(Product)
            .where(Product.id == product_id)
            .options(
                selectinload(Product.variants),
                selectinload(Product.reviews),
            )
        )
        result = await self.db.execute(stmt)
        product = result.scalar_one_or_none()
    
        if product is None:
            raise NotFoundError(f"Product with id '{product_id}' not found.")
    
>       return ProductRead.model_validate(product)
